=== Sheet: RJM Activity Fact View ===
1. View Name - RJM_ACTIVITY_FACT_V
3. View Schema Name - SSDS_CUSTOM_CONSUMER_DAL_OWNER
5. Table Functional Description - Activity for RJ Investment Management consumers
6. Filter Criteria -  from SSDS_DAL_OWNER.ACTIVITY_FACT_V  a,
SSDS_DAL_OWNER.ARRANGEMENT_MANAGED_ACCOUNT_SUBDIMENSION_V b
where b.MONEY_MANAGER_CODE = 'RJM'
and a.ARRANGEMENT_ID= b.ARRANGEMENT_ID
and a.TRADE_DATE + INTERVAL '23:59:59' HOUR TO SECOND BETWEEN b.EFFECTIVE_DATE and b.END_DATE
Logic if necessary: All fields - same as provisioned by Activity Fact View

=== Sheet: ETL Notes ===
The grain of this fact table is one row per transaction
The grain of this fact table is at TXN level.
The APA table has 4 types of APAs - cash, security, cash info, security info.  
In Activity Fact, We consider Cash, Cash Info  & Security records.
We exclude Security Info and Cash Info records from Activity Fact, because we can not have duplicate TXN ids to exist in Activity Fact table.
Mapping logic of various APA types:
ccal_repl_owner.txn t
join ccal_repl_owner.apa ap ON ap.exec_id = t.txn_id
join ccal_repl_owner.cl_val cv ON cv.cl_val_id = ap.apa_tp_id
APA.APA_TP_ID = CL_VAL.CL_VAL_ID
CASE	WHEN CL_VAL.CL_VAL_CODE between 'APACSH01' and 'APACSH78'  THEN 'APACASH'
	WHEN CL_VAL.CL_VAL_CODE between 'APACSH80' and 'APACSH99'  THEN 'iAPACSH'
WHEN CL_VAL.CL_VAL_CODE between 'APASEC01' and 'APASEC78' THEN 'APASEC'
WHEN CL_VAL.CL_VAL_CODE between 'APASEC80' and 'APASEC99' THEN 'iAPASEC' 
If transaction has only informational APAs, i.e. APA types have codes 80..99, load the transaction (APA attributes will remain blank)
A TXN can have (1 or Many) APAs
An APA can have (0 or Many) FIPs (i.e. Fees)
To determine the APA type, the APA_TP_ID needs to be decoded and the coded value parsed, like this:
ccal_repl_owner.apa ap
join ccal_repl_owner.txn t ON  ap.exec_id = t.txn_id
join ccal_repl_owner.cl_val cv ON cv.cl_val_id = ap.apa_tp_id
WHERE cv.cl_scm_id = '7'
APACASH :
Check for regexp_like(cv.cl_val_code,'^APACSH[0-7][0-9]')
For a Transaction, 
If only one record exists then consider that record.
If 2 records exists ( 
     If (one record is 'APACSH04' & other is 'APACSH11') 
          then consider skip 'APACSH04' record and load 'APACSH11' but use the values to
          (1) calculate aggregated value from APA.TXN_AMT fields from 'APACSH04' and 'APACSH11' and store it in Cash Transaction Amount and Cash System base currency amount
          (2) populate sales charge attributes from 'APACSH04' for 5 attributes (Sales Charge Rate Multiplier Number, Sales Charge Rate, Sales Charge Rate Type Code, Sales Charge Rate Type Id, Sales Charge Rate Type Name)
     else Drop those 2 records exception entire transaction
)

APASEC :
Check for cl_val_Code like '^APASEC[0-7][0-9]' THEN consider as 'Security' record.

iAPASEC/iAPACSH:
Refer to below section for further filter criteria on iAPASEC/iAPACSH. Applicable to both iAPACSH and iAPASEC.
Product Information: (Security source CUSIP, Security Product Id, Security CIRD Product Id, Security Option Symbol, Symbol, ISIN, Product Composite Description, Product Short Name, Product Description)
If there is atleast 1 APASEC, consider above fields from that APASEC
If there is an iAPASEC but no APASEC, consider above fields from iAPASEC

Source Effective Date:
If there is only iAPASEC or only iAPACSH, grab source effective date from the iAPASEC/iAPACSH
If there is atleast 1 APASEC or APACSH, grab source effective date from that APASEC/APACSH
Updates from below user names should be skipped by main process (Product Backlog Item 1937973: Skip Activity updates from additional usernames)
CCAL_PKG_TXN_RECON_REPL (EOD CCAL Recon Replay)
PERF_MAP_CF_MASTER_STG_PROC (Cash Flow Generation)
CCAL_PKG_TXN_POS_RECON_STS_UPD (EOD CCAL Recon)
CCAL_PERF_PKG_CF_MSTR_LOAD_RJTRST  (Cash Flow Generation)
CCAL_PKG_TXN_POS_RECON (EOD CCAL Recon)
CCAL_PKG_TXN_RECON_RJTRUST_1 (EOD CCAL Recon)
PERF_PKG_CF_MSTR_LOAD (Cash Flow Generation)
CCAL_PKG_TXN_RECON_SHADOW_1 (EOD CCAL Recon)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_1 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_2 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_3 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_4 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_5 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_6 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_7 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_8 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_9 (Activity Reclassification)
CCAL_PKG_LOAD_TXN_AY_CL_10 (Activity Reclassification)
Update Trade Cancelled Flag on original trade when cancellation arrives (Product Backlog Item 2030710: Add columns available in DWH and missing in Lighthouse for Trade Activity)
